      <div class="card__wrapper">
       <div class="card__content">
        <div class="card__tag" data-tax-tag="Vietnamese">
        </div>
        <span class="card__title">
         <span class="card__underline">
          Easy Wok-Kissed Beef Pho
         </span>
        </span>
        <p class="card__text">
         Homemade beef pho on a weeknight? YES! With a few shortcuts, this quick Vietnamese beef pho is ready in under and hour. Searing the beef in a hot skillet also adds great flavor!
        </p>
        <div class="comp showcase-hero__subtext mntl-block" id="showcase-hero__subtext_1-0">
